Pho usabonwa yini uMabhunu lapho?  Useshiye imoto laphaya ngasethilomu ukuze angene lapha phakathi kwesixuku.
Wathi esephindela emotweni, wamuzwa ekhuluma yedwana ethi:
"Uyangizwa-ke loBaldwin wabo lapho ngihamba khona?  Aze amtshele noVuyisile ukuthi zibuyile izinduku ngoba nabakubo bazoke baluzwe lolusizi angizwisa lona ngenkathi ngiseMnambithi.  Azifange-ke ngamvunye?"
Akaphindanga akalubeke unyawo lwakhe uMabhunu esibhedlela.  Indaba wazethukisa nje uma eseyixoxelwa uMaSithole lona abaqashe naye amakamelo kwaMadondo.








113

9. Ikhubalo Lenhlanhla.

Ngisho noma esemncane uMndayiza, esalandela amathole, wayebonakalisa uthando olungavamile lwemithi yesiNtu.  Wabekhonze ikakhulukazi imithi yokulutha, neyokuloya ngisho neyokukhunkula imbala.
. Wawumthola exoxa aze agamanxe ngezigqabo, izikhafulo namafutha ajulileyo ezilwane ahlonishwa ngisho nayizinyanga uqobo.

Engani ngisho nakhona lapha ekhaya kubo, emzini kaNdimande benoMaMbhele, wake wabenzela ezibukwayo bengazelele lutho?
Akuthi nje langa-lithize, uMndayiza ezelusele wona amathole akwabo eduzane nomuzi, bese ebona abafana abayintanga yakhe nabangaphezuywana bezidlalela ezansana nokhalo beciba insema, wabe uyasuka naye eseqonda kubo.  Omdala phela ukhangwa wukuthi baphethe izinkande kucitshwa yona insema.  Usethi makayobakhombisa ukuthi yena unemba kanjani ngenxele lakhe.  Nebala wathi angafika, zaqala manje ukwehla izihlathi kulabafana bakwaNdlovu nabakwaXulu abadala kunaye lokhu bebekhombisa ubungcweti babo ekunembeni.  Kepha kuthe uma efika umfo kaMaviyo, badlela ogageni.
Uma esethole lelosasasa lodumo uMndayiza, khohlwiyane yindaba yamathole sekumnandi phela ukuba elokhu enconywa ukuthi yena olwakhe ukhande kalukhi phansi.  Yena uyinemba ngisho noma igijima ngelingakanani ijubane insema kanti futhi akadingi nokuba seduzane nayo; uyikhomba nje kube kanye nakanjani uzoyihlaba.
Indaba leyo yokuthi konje ubeluse amathole, waze nje wayikhumbula ngelikade.  Wathi eqambe ethi qala-qala, nankaya amathole kade esezishonele konina lapho onondlini bese bekhalela ngakhona sebezisenga.  Uyaqambe uyafika, kade okungamathole sekwenyisile konina sekuzitshakadulela kungasabanake nakubanaka onina laba asebezilalele phansi

sebetshisa.
Wake wasenga-ke uNdinande ngalelolanga?  Phinde.  Engani
114
zontathu izinkomazi uzibonele yena ngamehlo ngenkathi sezenyisa.

Wathi esathi khekhekhe eziqhuba uMndayiza ezozingenisa esibayeni ukuze uyise asenge, wamemeza kuqala yena uNdimande wathi makasale esewayeka amathole konina.  Yena, into kuphela okufanele ukuba ayenze, wukuba ayolanda isitilobho babonane naye laphaya emva kwendlu.
Wamenzani-ke ngaso isitilobho ezinqeni nasemhlane uNdimande lowo?  Wawungaphika ukuthi ushaya amathumbu akhe ngoba wamshiya izinqana lezi kusengathi bezishiswa ngensimbi nasemhlane lapha nasemahlombe, kuxabalazile imivimbo eminye yaze yadabuka yopha igazi ngoba phela nayo lendoda enguMaviyo inenhliziyo elukhuni satshe.  Nalaba abamsolayo bemnuka ukuthi uyindoda ehamba-hambayo ebusuku, ungeze wamphikela ngoba nakhona lapha komakhelwane uma indoda ike yahilizisana naye, ngendaba yemngcele noma kambe uma kone impahla esifeni sakhe, kuyolinywa kane noma kahlanu bengabhekani engakaxoli uMaviyo.  Angisayiphathi-ke laba abake badazelane naye inkani ngoba indoda nayo yethembe izikhwama zayo, uyokwethuka sebemlandula lowo engasabikwanga nakubikwa ukuthi uyagula, kwasha kwacima.
Wamtalabha wamtalabha-ke ngalelolanga uMndayiza kwaze kwalamula yena uMaMbhele lapho uMndayiza esekhale empongoloza waze washa izwi uyise emhlalele ngaso isitilobho kanti umnyathele ngolungakanani lona unyawo ngenkathi sona isibhaxu sikhala lapha emhlane, emahlombe nakuzona iziqana lezi. Umshaya nje uyathetha lomuntu onguyise uyabalisa ,uyaqalekisa,uyasonga kunjeya.

'Hawu kodwa Ndimande sewungaze ingane uyikhiphe umphefumulo ngenxa nje yendaba yobisi?  Uma ngabe awukadeli, sala sewubulala mina okungcono ... kunini kodwa umqalile uMndayiza?  Kanti kuwena alisaxhoshwa yini libhekile?"

Washo uMaMbhele esithi hlwi isitilobho leso nakhu umzume wamvelela ngasemuva.  Pho, uyavinyelela yini?  Ungathi wena ubhula amabele.

Kwaba wukuphunyula kwakhe-ke njalo lapho uMndayiza wasubatha ngejubane ephaphatheka eyoshona ezihlableni elokhu ezihlikihla zona izinqana lezo ebalekela lendlondlo enguyise.

115

"Wenzani MaMbhele?  Manje sewuqala lomkhuba wakho wokuba uyone lengane ngokuyivuna uyikhulumele ngisho noma yonile?" sekufutheka yena uNdimande efikelwa amalimi usethukuthele manje usemnyama ngenkani sekungqangqa ngisho nodebe lolu lwakhe olukhulukazi.  Ungefunga ukuthi nezulu uyaliphuma.
'Mameshane!  Yona lengane oyikhulumelayo, ngekabani uma ingesiyo eyami?  Angikhumbuli nakancane ufika lapha emzini kamaphithi uqhuba ingane mhla uzochanguza - angikhumbuli nakancane!" Washo enxapha omdala esecanasa kancane esebheke endlini lapho ebeshiye isichitshana kumancishana.

"Usho kahle phela ngoba nakhu ngakufica uhlezi naye loMndayiza osewufuna ukumbulala ngezandla sengathi ubulele umuntu.  Sewuze umshaye kangaka umshayela nje indaba yobisi?  Sewungaze umshaye ngesitilobho-ke pho, baba?  Uma ingane yonile, bewunani ukhe uswazana lompetshisi uyithi -thwasu ezithweni kube kuphela ukuze ingane ikuhlothwasu

niphe ingakwesabi?  Ngiyazisa unenhliziyo yomthakathi!" Washo uMaMbhele eshaya izandla eyosithela exhibeni.  Naye hela uhambela kujana ngoba uyalwazi ulaka lwalesixhwa-
nguxhwangu sendoda yakhe uma sesithukuthele.  UNdimande angamswica nangani nje angase ayithole, kuphele ngalokho.  Ubani yena?
Kungathi esatshwa ngisho yilamadoda akhelene nawo; nawo ayawakhetha amazwi uma esuke eqondene naye ngoba nasembokodweni bayamenqena.  Ukhona yini umuntu ofuna ukuba kwendulelwe phezu kwakhe izwe lingaka nje?
Uthe angasiminya isicathulo leso, lase lehla igwebu lolaka.  Ngisho akaphendule.
UMndayiza laze lashona engabonwa lapha egcekeni waduba ngisho nokudla imbala.  Inhliziyo yakhe ibomvu okwegazi futhi igaya izibozi uma ezwa leminjunju eshoshozela lapha emhlane nasezinqeni.  Phela ngenhliziyo embi, akungatshazwa ukuthi lwefuza imbiza.  Waze wayoncengwa wunina sekuzolalwa ukuba abuye azolala.  Wathi noma ethi uyamncenga ukuthi akakhe kanye lapha emthameni obandayo igugu lakhe, wenqaba waphetha.  Esikhundleni salokho waqala phansi ukusikhihla futhi isililo nakhu phela yiwona lamasi asecishe wabulawa nguyise ngenxa yawo.

116

Kwaze kwasa ecabanga engaqedi ukuthi konje angayibuyisela kanjani leminjunju kuyise omzalayo.  Akusekho ngisho nokuncane ukuzisola lapha kuye ukuthi nguye obesephutheni yingakho nje uyise eseze amshaye ashiye lona ulimi ukuba aze ayixoxele amagwababa mhla ewafica esigcakini echobana!  Wasonga ukuthi ngamhla wakhula naye wabanamandla, uyoze amkhumbuze uyise leyomivimbo yesitilobho.

Ekuseni ngakusasa kwabonwa nguye ukuthi sekusile.  Kwaba nje wukubona ukuthi sekuyakhanya ngaphandle, wabe ephuma njalo aye athi tshobe ehlathini leli elingakwesobunxele somuzi.  Phela wakhe ehlanzeni uMaviyo.  Wathi ebuya lapho wabe eyikhe ngezinkani imbabazane.  Wathi nje efika nayo wabe ehleka yedwa nakhu phela useyitholile lento abeyicabanga ubusuku bonke.  Wabe edumela ijazi likayise eselikhatha ngayo imbabazane ngaphakathi emfolomini.  Waqinisa lapha emakhwapheni nasesiphikeni salo ijazi leli likayise.  Wathi angadela kahle ukuthi nasemhlane lapha ulikhathe wenele, wase elibuyisela futhi emgibeni lapho belivele lilenga khona yena wabe ebuyela esiphukwini sakhe esezilalisa sengathi ubengazange akaye ndawo.

Phela nakhona lapha ekhaya kuyaziwa ukuthi yena uze aphunyelwe yilanga futhi lize liqophe engakavuki.  Engani kwasho yena uyise ukuthi akafuni ukuba izinkomo zakhe zivulelwe ekuseni ngoba uma zidla utshani busenamazolo zibanenyongo zingenwe nawumbendeni kalula.  Waphindela kuzona iziphuku zakhe wazilalisa-ke ezembozile okomuntu impela ozumekile kanti yena uyayazi into ayilindile.  Engani wazi kamhlophe ukuthi uyise ngenkathi evuka, nakanjani uzothi nje angaphuma ezingutsheni zokulala, abe eligqoka lelijazi lakhe phezu kwebheshu bese ecanalsa kancane eseyobuka uchibi lwezinkomo zakhe esibayeni lapho lusaziguqele ekuseni lwetshisa ngoba phela lendoda enguNdimande yefuyile.  Ezayo izinkomo lezi zibulala inyoka uma ziphuma esibayeni.  Lapha ezinkabini zejoka, unezipani ezintathu ehleli nje, kanti-ke ngisho nesesine siyaphuma nje kalula uma sekukubi.

UMndayiza ulele nje, akalele nakulala; ulindele nje ukuba uyise enze phela inhlayenza yakhe leyo yokuba ayonumuza ayohlola imfuyo yakhe esibayeni ngoba lokhu ukwenza ngi-

117

sho noma izulu lina imbala.  UMndayiza ulokhu elivezile iso
phansi kwesiphuku.
Ngelikade amuzwe uyise esezamula kuhle okwebhubesi; phela yena uma esuke ezamula ungefunga ukuthi kuzamula ubhova noma ibhubesi lilambile.  Dukuduku, awabone amaqikolo ezinyawo zikayise seziqonde emgibeni lapho lilenga khona ijazi likayise.  Kwaba nje wukuba alibeke emahlombe, sase sisukile isidumo lesi abesilindele.  Wathi eqambe eyifaka imikhono lapha ezingalweni, yathi imbabazane kangenziwa njalo mina.  Kwaba seyisizakele lapho izomthola emakhwapheni lapha nasentanyeni - izindawo ezithambileyo.  Emhlane lapha kwaba sengathi uthelwe ngeziqanda seyimbabela imbabazane yansondo; pho ubeyifake ngezinkani naye uMndayiza lowo.
Walikhumula sengathi uyasha uNdimande uma seyimkhungethe wonke umzimba imbabazane wabhongisa okwenkunzi yesibhunu yenkomo ebiza omaphithi abamzalayo wena omuzwayo ungaze ucabange ukuthi ubhekene nendlondlo enophaphe emvimbele endleleni kanti akaphethe nduku akusekho nokuyibalekela!  Wathi angalikhumula waye walitshinga laphaya kude naye wabe ezenwaya ngazozombili.  Ayisababike lapho imbabazane sewungathi uyayibanga ngokuzenwaya lokho lapha emakhwapheni nasemhlane ngoba waze wazihhubha ngensika yendlu ngoba nakhu isandla asikwazi ukufinyelela emhlane.  Uma uke uyibone ingulube izenwaya ukhwekhwe, sewubona yena-ke uMaviyo ngalelolanga!
'Hawu!  Yini kwenzenjani yise kaKhethiwe walahla ijazi phansi?" sekumangala uMaMbhele lapho ezithela kulona ijazi eliyigugu elikhulu elaba yisibizo saseMadungeni lapho bendisela khona uKhethiwe, inkosazana lena enguMafungwase lapha kuyise.  Alicoshe ethi uyambheka uyise wabantwana, nanguya manje usezigudla ngobonda lwendlu uyazenwaya nangezandla ungefunga ukuthi ukhwelwe yimbuzi-beyishuka!
"Usabuza kona ukubuza MaMbhele?  Phuthuma kewubheke ukuthi asikho yini lesicabu esinesihlungu laphaya ejazini ngoba sekub aba wonke umzimba selokhu ngike ngalibeka emzimbeni wami ijazi leli!" Usho njalo uyazihhubha lomuntu seyiphele nya inkani.  Nomame aliphuthume aphumele nalo phandle ukuze asibheke isilwanyana leso.

118

"Hawu!  Baba, kanti ukhuluma nje sewugcwele isihlungu wonke umzimba!" Kubabaza yena uMaMbhele lapho ebona ukuthi sekugcwele isihlungu wonke umhlane lapha kumyeni wakhe.  Phela uNdimande uma eke wathola umkhemezelo, uqubuka isihlungu sekhambi wonke umzimba.  Kepha ngoba alizange keline nje futhi kanti ubengakaphumeli naphandle uNdimande, pho kungabe lesihlungu sivuswe yini.
"Nkosikazi, sekubaba wonke umzimba sondela nawe ungenwaye lapha emhlane ngafa - bo!" kuzikhalela umnumzane womuzi ezenwaya ebheke phambili.
Kwenzeka nje konke lokhu, uzithulele uMndayiza uyabukela sekuthi makaqhume yinsini uma eyizwa lendoda enguyise izikhalela ibalisa.  Kanti naye uyabuzwa ubuhlungu?  Usesho nje ngenhliziyo uthi: 'Ashosho phela!  Mudle kudla kwakhe!!  Ubani obewumshaya ngesitilobho izolo?  Uyangizwa-ke?"
Waze wazivukela nje ngelikade uMndayiza wazembathela isiphuku sakhe wayoziphumela ngomnyango eyohlala esigcakini ngoba usecishe waphubuka wahleka lapho eyibona indoda enguyise seyisele nensudi yesele ibhokelwe yimbabazane selisele phansi ibheshu nezinjobo!  NoMaMbhele usebamba eyeka ethi uyayilamula lenkinga eseyivele ukuba lelijazi eliyigugu kangaka selingaze lilahlwe nje phansi kanjeya!
Laze laphela lonke lelosonto njalo ekuseni uMaMbhele avuke ijazi lelo ayoleneka ngemfilomu engilazini.  UNdimande yena uselesabisa okwenyoka.  Usexolele ukuba kuthi uma eyohlola izinkomo zakhe, embathe wona umbhalala wakhe wokulala.  UMndayiza yena, uthi nje angalibona ijazi lelo lenekiwe, kuthi akaqhume yinsini.
Ngisho ukuba kebasole abazali ukuthi kungabe uMndayiza unolwazi ngalento eseyenze uyise ukuba azile ijazi lakhe leli athi uma eligqokile umbone ehamba kancane echiza.
Zadlula izinyanga ezintathu kwenzekile kokhu; nakhu sekufika uZondo ezozikhalela lapha kuNdimande ngomfana wokwelusa.  Lomfana obekade ebelusela leminyaka emine eyedlule useshiyile waya kosebenza eziMobeni zabelungu laphaya ngasolwandle.  Wathi uma ebancenga uZondo kwaze kwezwela kuMaMbhele base bevuma ukuthi uMndayiza angayihlanganisa imihlambi yomibili ngoba futhi nakhu imizi yakhelene.

119

"Maqondana nenkokhelo yomfana, kangazi ukuthi sizovumelana yini ekubeni ahole inkomo yoboya njalo uma kuphela unyaka." Sekusho uNdimande uma seliphumile lapha kuMaMbhele ukuthi yena akaboni usizo lukaMndayiza lapha ekhaya.
"Sekungaba yinkomo impela Ndimande?  Engani uyasho nawe ukuthi umfana kuzothi uma kulusuku lwediphu nami ngimphelekezele ngoba zingamehlula uma ezihlanganisile?" sekuzikhalela uZondo.
"Uxolo Mthiyane, sengathi sizoxabana nje singakafiki ndawo," sekusho uNdimande.  "Manje uma sewuzongishayela wena umthetho emzini wami, futhi ngalomfana wami, okungcono asivele siyeke.  Akumina engixakekile futhi angizange ngiye kofuna lutho emzini wamuntu."
"Hawu, kahle phela yise kaKhethiwe, wase ukhuluma sengathi uncikisele nje?" sekusho uMaMbhele ngoba uyamazi umyeni wakhe nenhliziyo yakhe yobuwele - sengathi kwakuphikiwe ukuthi wabe eliwele nodadewabo lona owendele kwaHlongwa eBhobhobho ngaphesheya kweNdonyane.
"Impela Ndimande ngiyazikhalela ukuthi ningizwele bakithi ngoba mina abami abantwana basebancane kakhulu.  Okungcono sesingakhulumela khona etholeni maqondana nenkokhelo." Sekusho uZondo.  Uyasho nje ngenhliziyo ukuthi impela enethunga ayisoze yasengelwa phansi.
UMndayiza uma seyimdlile kanjalo inkatha yokwelusa imihlambi yomibili, konke sekuhlelwe kahle ngokuvumelana phakathi komakhelwane bobabili.  Nebala konke kwahamba kahle konke ngoba namadlelo ahlumile kanti nezimoba zabeLungu zibuqamamana.  Usizo uze aludinge nje kuphela ngosuku lwangoLwesine - usuku lwediphu.  Nakhona lapho bahamba nje naye uZondo usezoziyela ematshwaleni namanye amadoda.  Sekuyoze kufike uLwesine olulandelayo kube yisona leso futhi.  Kanti-ke, nangaphandle nje kwalokho, uMndayiza udla ekhaya zonke izinsuku futhi ulala khona.  Ebusika, nawo amadiphu eqisa amasonto kuthi futhi uma izulu lina, akudishwa.
Kwahamba kahle waphela unyaka welanywa ngomunye.  Ekupheleni konyaka wakhe ebusika, abakwaZondo sebezokhomba ithole lapha esibayeni ukuthi yilo abaholela ngalo

120

uMndayiza nokho lingaze lesulwa lapha ebhukwini lakwaZondo.

Uyabuka njalo uMndayiza uzithulele.  Ayikamkhohli phela nendaba leyo ake ayenziwa nguyise ngesitilobho.  Yikho nje engajahe nokuba izinkomo lezi zakhe zisheshe zesulelwe lapha kuyise.  Iyahamba nje iminyaka, naye uyabala.
Ingxabano yasuka nje okomlilo osuswa yinhlansi kanti uzoshisa amazwe.  Nakhona lapha phakathi kwabakwaZondo nabakwaNdimande uchuku lwasuka nje ngentwana encane: ngonyaka wesibili babekhombe isithole unkomishi bathi yisona abasiholela uMndayiza.  Ngalonyaka-ke unkomishi lowo asuke azibule, futhi azibule ngesithole.
Izindaba uMmndayiza uyazithuthela lapha kunina uMaMbhele. Kuthe uma uMaMbhele ezwa ukuthi isithole sikaMndayiza sizibule ngesithole esinye, wase ethi kuhle uMndayiza athi ufuna ukuba zesulelwe ebhukwini lakubo zonke lezinkomo esezibiza yena.  Empeleni uMaMbhele wayesejahe ukuba nabo bavube lapha ezinkomeni zikaMndayiza.
Wasizakala lapho uNdimande nakhu phela uNkomishi wazala yedwa kwathi zonke ezinye izithole zalapha kwaZondo kanye nezimazi imbala, zaphunza.  Nabo-ke abakwaZondo base bekhalela kuyena uNkomishi ukuze nabo basenge.  Waqala kanjalo-ke umbango namazwi angabe asabamnandi phakathi kukaMaMbhele benoMaNgobese - umkaZondo.  Pho, ubani ongazi ukuthi uma udaba seluze lwangenwa abantu besifazane, ngeke kusabuye kulunge lutho?
Ngisho naye uMndayiza uqobo lwakhe usekhombisa ngokusobala ukuthi akasagculisekile kangako ngoba ngisho nasekuseni akasenzi njengakuqala lapho wayevuka akuseni ayovulela ezakwaZondo bese ezihlanganisa nalezi zakubo; muva nje uqala avulele lezi zakubo azishonise emfundeni.  EzakwaZondo zona useyoze azivulele lezi zakubo sezesuthi osekukhombisa khona ukuthi manje useshisa umbango.  Loluhlevana lwezinkulumo lwase lubuye lwandiswa nayilendaba yokuphunza kwazo zonke ezakwaZondo izinkomazi emveni kokuba kuke kwabanezinkulumana.  Baqala manje ukuba bakhulumele phansi omakhelwane.
Sebeyasho nalaba abanye abafana ukuthi lesinonseyana esinguMndayiza izinkomazi zakwaZondo ubezishaya ngomazwende yingakho nje ziphunzile.  Loluswazana lwakhe lu-

121

kamazwende uthi uma esezozivalela, alugqibe khona lapha esibayeni sakwaZondo bese eziphathela nje indukwana enganakekile.  Indaba phela kayihlali phansi ukuthi yena Mndayiza lowo unemishana ayiphuzisa lezi ezakubo zodwana.  Useke waphahluka kaningana nalapha kontanga yakhe ukuthi yena uma ethanda, angaziphuzisa umuthi othile ezakhe zizale izithole zodwa.  Waze washo nokuthi ngisho noma isithole leso sesibambile, uyakwazi yena ukusimisela sizale isithole uma eseziphuzise lomuthi wakhe.  Bathi uma lendaba beyixoxa emakhaya koyise, basukumela phezulu abanumzane bezozidelela nebala kwaba njengawo amagama enkehli.
Omunye umnumzane babhejelana ngenkomazi yakhe eyabe seyilamanise amaduna kwaze kwakathathu.  Kwathi eseyiphuzise lomuthi wakhe uMndayiza, yaqala-ke ukwelamanisa izithole wabe uyayithatha njalo imbuzikazi kulomnumzane njengoba babebhejelane ngayo.  Lomuthi wakhe wodumo, uma besho, bathi uthakwa ngomhlapho wevondwe nezinso zephithi neminye-ke imithi embiwayo.
Waqala-ke manje uMndayiza ukuba yindaba eGudwini.  Nakhona lapha ekwaluseni umfica engungwe abanumzane bemizi yabo nakhu phela omdala unomona akafuni ukuba noyise athole usizo ngaye.  Uthi uma esekhokha, amshayele nje imbuzi azoyethula kubo sengathi uyithengelwe abakwaZondo.  Wadelisa abanumzane abaningi impela babamba ongezansi bemangaliswe ukuthi kungabe ulwazi lwemithi yesibaya uluthathephi lokhu uyise bamazela ekubetheleni izulu, izikhafulo zezibhobo nemithi yokuthakatha namaqondo kuphela.  Kulena yesibaya akazi ngisho iboza leli lokusiza.
Kusenjalo, watshela abangane bakhe ukuthi ngalowonyaka ezakhe izinkomo zizozala amalunga wodwa ngenkathi zikhwelwa.  Kwadingiseka nje ukuthi angakusho kanjani lokho ngoba ngisho nasediphu ayikho inkunzi elunga.  Kepha akubanga njalo?
Uma sebeqaphelisisa, kwakuthi uma lezi zakubo zizophuza, afake induku enamagabelo amhlophe n'amnyama bese kuba nebhodlela lakhe elithelwa lapho kuzobe kuphuza lezi zakubo zodwa seziphuze zonke lezi ezinye zemizi.  Ziyothi zingaphuza ezakhe bese eyikhipha futhi indukwana yakhe leyo ayifihle ekwazini kwakhe useyoze ayifake futhi ngakusasa sekuphuza zona ezakubo.

122

Kwathi futhi uma esephusa uNkomishi, nakhu eselandelwa yizinkunzi kabusha, yaqala phansi futhi indaba yokuba abakwaNdimande babelesele ukuthi phela sekuyisona isikhathi sokuba 'zibuye emasisweni.' Manje sekukhulunywa indaba yokuba abakwaNdimande besulelwe izinkomo eziyisithupha uma sekubalwa nezibulikazi likaNkomishi kanti abakwaZondo bona bathi naso isithole leso sikaNkomishi siyinkomo ngokwaso.
Washa-ke lapho lowombango kwashisa phansi ngoba udaba lolo lwaze lwayosingathwa wumnumzane esigcawini sekumangele phela uMaviyo ethi nakhu uZondo esenqaba nezinkomo ezasetshenzelwa wumfana wakhe iminyaka emihlanu.
Uma seliqulwa ebandla, uZondo yena ubambelele ephuzwini lokuthi lesithole esizalwa wuNkomishi usibala njengenkomo ngokwaso njengoba nakhu sazalelwa emqubeni wesibaya sakhe.  Aqhube lapho azikhalele ngokuthi okungenani yena ubengavuma ukuba ashaye izinkomo ezintathu lapha esibayeni bese kuthi lezi ezimbili kube yizinkomo zemali.
Kwathi akamudle amfele uNdimande uma ezwa lelo lenkokhelo yemali.  Washo nokusho ukuthi kanti uZondo wayeze emzini wakhe ngoba nakhu ezomgabisela ngemali yakhe yini?
'Mina elami lokugcina, ngelokuthi uZondo uma engavumi ukunginikeza izinkomo zami zonhlanu nethole likaNkomishi, angavele ayeke phansi angakhokhi ngisho nenkukhu kuphele ngalokho." Sekusho yena uNdimande lapho eseqephuza ekhulu-ma eneka izandla phambi kwebandla.
Likhuze lapho ibandla ngoba useyasonga, uyaqalekisa ukhomba phezulu.
'Kanti-ke bakithi ibandla malingakhohlwa phela ukuthi nguyena uZondo owangisukela ngizihlalele emzini wami ngingafune lutho lwamuntu.  Kanti wayeze ngoba eqonde khona ukuba angigone angenze inhlekisa?  Uma engafuni ukusigcina isethembiso sakhe leso, angavele ayeke phansi kuyozikhanyela."
Kwathula kwathi cwaka ebandla ngoba nakhu ukhuluma abuye angunuze uMaviyo ngenkathi sekukhuluma uZondo ethalalisa.  Pho lapha ebandleni ukhona yini ongafisa ukuba agxambukele kuloludaba uma owakhe umbono uphikisana nalona obekwa uyena uMaviyo ngokwakhe.  Baphi oNyengelezi noSigwegwe abake baphikisana naye uMaviyo lo?  Bama-

123

thambo-mhlophe - silima phezu kwabo, mntanomuntu!
"Wona unyaka wakhe umfana uphela nini?" sekubuza yena umnumzane nakhu sengathi ibandla likhoshobele akekho ofuna ukukhuluma nje agqashule selokhu lungenile esigcawini ngezithebe loludaba phakathi kukaZondo benoNdimande.
"Mina.ngokwami, unyaka womfana ngiwubala kusukela ngesikhathi kwendulelwa ngoba ngikhumbula ukuthi umfana wamthatha izinkomo kade ziqoqwa kade zidla amahlanga." Leyo kube yimpendulo kaNdimande.  Kulelophuzu bayavumelana bobabili noZondo.
Wancenga encengile bandla uZondo ekubeka ngokusobala ukuthi yena wabe engaqonde ngxabano kuphela nje uyazikhalela nasebandleni lilonke ukuthi isimo sakhe sibucayi ngenxa yokuthi ezinye izinkomo zakhe zibulawe wumbendeni ngakho-ke uyazikhalela ukuthi lingawa ijoka uma zingase zesulwe kanye kanye lezinkomo futhi kade engakuhlinzekile lokho yingakho nje ezincengela ukuthi okungenani uNdimande akayemukele imali.
Pho uqondene nomfokaMiphitha - uxamu kavinjelwa ongezwa makhambi uma yena into seyishilo, useyishilo.
Yazukuzwa-ke leyondaba engezwa nakuzwa uNdimande.  Ekugcineni umnumzane waze walikhipha yena elokuthi uZondo okungenani makakhokhele uNdimande ama-R75 uma ngabe uyalihlonga leliduna akhala ngalo ukuthi kungawa isipani uma ngabe lesulelwa kuNdimande.
Kwehlukanwa lapho uNdimande esemnyama kuhle okwezulu lihloma.  Usakhala isililo saleliduna elimphunyuke emlonyeni ngoba naye ngokwakhe ubeligasele ngamehlo abomvu ukuze naye aphembe isipani sesine - imali uyayihola ngokulimela abantu laba abangefuyile.  Uqashe abantu bokubalimela yena eze nje ngoba ezonquma imali kube kuphela.
Kwaba sengathi selidume ledlula'uma-ke sezize zesulwa lezinkomo zikaMndayiza kanti abasabuzanga elangeni kumfokaMiphitha omnyama ngisho nenhliziyo yakhe.
Kwaba nje azesuliwe; isibaya sakwaZondo saqala kancane kancane ukuba simile imbuya njengosongo lolo olwenziwa wuNdimande mhla linqunywa komkhulu.
Izinkomo zaqala manje ukuba zephuke ubuphoqophoqo
zilandelana.  Uma inkomo ingephukanga nje obala, bazokwethuka nje sezibhokodana zodwana khona lapha esibayeni.  Kuyogcina ngokuba ize iqedelwe leyo elimeleyo.  Kudingeke nje ukuthi kungabe kwenzenjani ngoba ayikho inkomo entsha lapha esibayeni.  Wathi uma uZondo eyophenya emhlahlweni, basho into efanayo - ukuthi kwembelwa uphoqo lapha esibayeni yikho nje izinkomo zephuka kangaka ngoba ziweqa lapha empundwini uma ziphuma.  Ukuxabana lokhu kubangwa yiqeba leziqanda elathunyiselwa zona ukuba zizondane.
UNkomishi wathi nje efika esibayeni sakwaNdimande wabe elamanisa ngesinye futhi isithole.  UMndayiza waba nezinkomo nje eziyisithupha uma sekufike lezi azisebenze kwaZondo.  Ushintshisa nangezimbuzi lezi aziholelwa abanumzane ngokubamisela izibaya zabo.
Saqala manje isibaya sikaNdimande ukuba sinakeke kanti futhi ngisho nayo impahla ngokwayo yanonophala yancibilika yabiza umuntu ezihambela ngendlela.
UMndayiza welusa nje kanti futhi uzibambela mathupha ukuze laba abamfunayo bamthole kalula khona endle bangaze bayobonana noyise hleze aze anyonkele lapha esifeni sakhe ukuthi uhlanganisani nani lapha emakhambini.  Iselokhu ikhona leyansila yegqubu lenzondo phakathi kwakhe noyise.  Akakhohlwa ufana nesithole sendlovu - indaba yesitilobho uyikhumbula njalo uma esuke egeza ezwa imizizima elapha emhlane engasoze yaphela.
Dukuduku, wabe esethi kungabangcono isibaya sishintshwe endaweni yaso kwathi kulesi esisha wembela ihobosha empundwini wasibethela.  Kwathi lezi zakubo zaphuziswa ugobho kanti njalo ntambama zithunyiselwa ngodengezi lwamakhekheba ezinyosi ukuze zithandane futhi zizibuyele.  Zasuke zakhuluphala kunakuqala kanti nabantu kwaba sengathi sebetshelene befika bezomfuna ukuba azobaqinisela izibaya zabo.  Naye uMaviyo useqalile manje ukuba ayihloniphe indodana futhi kukhona nokuyesaba.
Kungabe lolulwazi lwamakhambi kungabe uMndayiza walutholaphi, lokhu zonke izinsuku ulala lapha ekhaya?  Sekuze kusho uMaMbhele ukuthi kunensizwa yempondo umfokafikeni oyaye afike lapha bahambe naye njalo ntambama nezimbo.  Lomfo usebenza kwaloliwe khona lapha eduzane.
Zanda izinkomo zikaMndayiza sagcwala isibaya sikaNdimande abantu bebhekile.  Phela manje sebeza nje udede bezomfuna ekhaya ukuba ayobethela aqinise izibaya zabo aze azimisele izimazi imbala.  Uma ehambile, kuzosala lona ikhehla leli elinguyise leluse nakhu futhi seligugile kanti selivamise nokuzibika.  Seyiphelile inkani manje.
Lapha balimela abantu kanti futhi bathengisa ngobisi emzini lena yabantu abangafuyile nakotisha laba abaqashe izindlu zokuhlala abangenankomo.
Kwaba nguyise manje osefuna umfana wokwelusa ngoba nakhu uMndayiza usekhulile kanti futhi isikhathi akasenaso sokwelusa ebizwa ebiziwe lapha emizini.
Wathi lapho eyikhomba intombi yenduna umadlala, washaya kulezi ezakhe zoboya kwaba yizibizo kuphela azikhokha ngemali.  Aziphelanga izinyanga eziyisithupha uMaMadlala eyingoduso zaziwushaya kumfokaMaviyo.
Emva kokushada-ke wabe eseyofuna umsebenzi kwaloliwe eduzane eMzumbe.  Wasebenza elala ekhaya nakhu futhi nalo ikhehla elinguMaviyo selivamise ukulaliswa yimikhuhlane nezilalo futhi engumuntu wephika uma ligqubuthele izulu.
Wathi uyophela unyaka uMaMadlala wabe ehluba ngoba lathi liyoshaya iPhasika wabe encelisa indodakazi.
Lapha emsebenzini nakhona wathi nje efika, waba yindabamlonyeni ngoba nalo udumo lwakhe lwase luhambe phambili kusukela koFairview, koMagogo, koMzumbe Home kuye kuyoshaya eMabheleni (Hibberdene) imbala.  Abanumzane sebefika nakhona lapha emsebenzini bezomfuna ukuba azobaqinisela izibaya zabo.
Wathi uphela unyaka wesibili esebenza, kwakumenela uMaviyo ukufa ekhaya basala bodwa manje oMaMandlala noninazala nendodakazi uma esemsebenzini uMndayiza.  Nokho, bakhona abantu laba bokusenga nabalimayo.  UMaMadlala yena unesivande lapho etshale khona imfino ayithengisayo.  Sekukhona nemithi asemethwese yona umkakhe ukuze kuthi uma befike engekho, akwazi ukubathakela.
Indaba eyacishe yamphatha kabana ngeyokuthi nangu uFikeni esebika ukuthi naye usefuna ukubuyela kwelakubo eFlagstaff.  Washiya emdonse ngendlebe ukuthi nakanjani aze alokhu exhumene naye ngezincwadi ukuze basizane.
Ikhubalo abe eligasele kakhulukazi uMndayiza ngaphezu kwaleli lemfuyo kwabe kuyikhubalo lenhlanhla leli abe elincothi uma engase athole lona ngeke ma kakhulu uFikeni uku

esadinga ukusebenza kumlungu ngoba imali iyozizela.
Waqhuba-ke lezozinyanga ezimbalwa lapha kwaloliwe uma esehambile uFikeni wase enza ihlambo likayise ngoba wabe eselindele ukuba kuphele isikhathi leso abesimisile.
Wathi angawuqeda umsebenzi lowo kayise, wase esula lapha kwaloliwe ngoba nakhu esehambile nomngane wakhe ebecobelelana naye amakhambi - yena uFikeni phela.  Ikhubalo leli lemfuyo liyamlethela imali ngempela ngoba uma kukhona okudingekayo, usebheka khona esibayeni athengise abangule iva lelo elimhlabile.  Ngisho naye uMaMadlala ngeke ehlulwa yilutho uma engase akathi hulukuqu akaye kothwasela lelikhubalo lenhlanhla koFikeni njengesivumelwane.
Bayabhalelana noFikeni sonke lesikhathi behlukana.  Dukuduku, wabe esevalelisa eselibhekise khona eMampondweni wasishiya sizikhalela isalukazi esinguMaMbhele ebathembisa

ukuthi uyobuya uma esephothule.
Waphela unyaka uMndayiza engabonwa kuleli laseMzumbe.  Ekupheleni konyaka lowo wake wathi qu ekhaya, ebuyele uKhisimusi nakhu futhi wayethole umbiko wokuthi unina aka-

philile kahle futhi ukhala ngaye.
Wafika kwawa inkabi umfo kaMaviyo nakhu phela ufike lapha eyisebenzile ngempela imali uMaMadlala kanti naye ngokwakhe usefunde ukuchathela inyoni.  Omame baphambana lapha belethe izingane zabo - iyangena imali ibheke phambili.  Waqeda amasonto amabili lawo wase evalelisa manje esebathembisa ukuthi useyoze abuye ebusika esebuya

unomphela.
Wathi uma esebuyele enyangeni emethwasisayo, yase imtshela ukuthi sekusele nje ukuba akayongeniswa esizibeni esinenkanyamba emakhanda amahlanu ukuze adumelane nayo ukuze kubonakale ukuthi unesibindi.  Uma esedlule lapho uyobe useqedile ngoba nakhu usenalo nekhubalo legwababa elingatholwa kalula.  Into esasele kuphela yiwona umdaka omhlophe nobuchopho benkunzi yamanzi.
Nayo lenyanga yabo benoFikeni ifike yamkhonza kakhulu ngoba bafike bacobelelana ngolwazi analo lwesiZulu nayo

yamthwesa lawa esiMpondo amakhambi.
'Mfo kaNdimande, uyozibonela wena imisebenzi yalelikhubalo unyaka ungakapheli," sekusho yona inyanga lena uma

127

sebexoxa ngalo lelikhubalo aligasele lenhlanhla.  'Ngiyakutshela ukuthi ngeke usamsebenzela umlungu ngoba imali iyozingenela nje okwamanzi uma unaso isibindi."

"Manje yisibindi sani lesi osishoyo?" sekubuza yena uMndayiza lumuthi heqe uvalo.

"Habe, siyadingeka isibindi uma ngabe uzifuna izinhlanhla.  Lelikhubalo ngeke lakusebenzela lutho uma ungafikanga walihlabisa walikhunga.  Uma ungakwenzanga lokho, liyokuphenduka libulale wena uqobo lwakho." sekusho uFikeni ngoba yena usabuya khona lapho esizibeni.
'Manje uthi likhungwa kanjani lona lelikhubalo?" asho akhombise ukwethuka lapho uMndayiza ngoba uke ezwe ukuthi eminye imithi ifuna ukuba abulale umuntu alikhunge ngegazi lakhe.
"Lelikhubalo ukuze likusebenzele, kuyodingeka ukuba ufike ulikhunge ngesibindi somuntu.  Uma lokho ungakwenzanga, ufile wena uqobo lwakho," sekusho inyanga uqobo lwayo.
"Uthi likhungwa ngesibindi somuntu?  Manje ngichazele kahle ngizwe kahle ukuze ngingenzi iphutha," sekusho yena uMndayiza efikelwa yifindo emphinjeni.  "Uthi kufuneka ngilikhunge ngesibindi somuntu onjani?"
"Engani ngiyakutshela nje ukuthi lomuthi ungakawungenisi ekhaya, kuyodingeka uqale uwukhunge ngesibindi somuntu oyigazi lakho - isihlobo sakho esiseduze futhi ozalana naso." Sekuchaza uFikeni ngoba uyambona ukuthi wethuke kakhulu.
"Kufuneka lowomuntu abeligazi nami?  Usho ukuthi yena umkami angeze alunga uma ngilihlabise yena?" Cha, uMndayiza wethuke kakhulu impela ngoba usehhema nje.  Bathi ukumbheka oFikeni nenyanga lena.  Bamfice ejuluka kancane nakhu phela yena ubethi nje yinto nje leyo elula ngoba angazingela lababantu abayimizulane ambulate maqede amcwiye isibindi leso kuphele ngalokho.  Manje kufuneka isibindi somuntu oligazi lakhe?
"Umkakho naye ulungile phela ngoba useyinsila yakho.  Empeleni, bewungabulala unyoko noma uyihlo bona asebezigugele noma kambe ingane yakho ukuze lezi ezinye zidle kahle lapha emhlabeni.  Naye umkakho ulungile ngoba phela naye usengumndeni wakwaNdimande." Sekuchaza uFikeni.  "Ungesabi mngane wami, ubona abantu benethezeka nje, basuke bedele lukhulu, mfana'kithi."

128

Cha athule isikhathi eside impela kubonakale ukuthi kulukhuni usazama ukukhetha lowo azomdela ukuba akhunge ngaye lelikhubalo lenhlanhla.
'Kanti-ke uma sewukwenzile lokho, ngisho nawe uqobo lwakho uyozibonela ukungena kwemali uma sewuwukhungile lomuthi," sekujobelela inyanga." Ngiyakuyala ukuthi ungalingi uwungenise lomuthi ekhaya ungakwenzile lokho ngoba lomuthi uyozihlabisa wona osapheni lwakho uma ungavukelanga wena uqobo lwakho.  Ungethande nawe ukuba lokho kwenzeke kuwe emva komsebenzi ongaka nezindleko osewungene kuzo.  Kanti wena kawufuni yini ukunethezeka ukhombe ngophakathi?"
"Ngethuswa yileli lokuthi ngisho nami uyongibulala uma ngingawukhunganga kanti-ke bese ngibone kahle ukuthi ngizo ..." kusho yena uMndayiza ngoba ubesacabanga sona isalukazi esinguMaMbhele ukuthi kungabangcono uma engaphumuza sona nakhu futhi sesasala sodwa.  Ngenhliziyo uyasho nje ukuthi makube bekusekhona uyise uMaviyo, ubengeke angabaza nakancane ukuba kube nguye akhunga ngaye lelikhubalo.  Uma engabulala uMaMadlala, angathi uzosala nobani badle lemali abayisebenzayo?  Futhi naye uMaMadlala ngokwakhe engani usembonile ukuthi uyindoda ngokwakhe engani wafika wayofaka ebhange ama-R350 imali esetshenzwe uyena uMaMadlala eyedwa?  Uma enikela ngoNomvula, indodakazi, yona lemali ayisebenzayo, iyoba ngekabani uma efa?
Uyena nje uMaMbhele ongafanela ukuba imudle lenkatha yokukhunga ikhubalo leli.

Lezozinyangana ezazisasele zaba wunyaka kuMndayiza.  Manje usabulala yini bona ubuthongo?  Kuze kuse ecabanga, ebamba eyeka ezama ukuhlaziya ukuthi konje wubani ozalweni okufanele ukuba amhlabise ikhubalo lakhe leli lenhlanhla yomcebo.  Abuye akhumbule udadewabo uKhethiwe hhayi-ke lapho avuke ahlale ngesinqe.  Kodwa yena umkhwenyawabo angambheka ngamaphi nje wona amehlo uma engasukela umuntu owalala siswini sinye na e kuMaMbhele?  Bona nje abashana bakhe angababheka athini azi kahle ukuthi bazintandane nje ngenxa yakhe?
Cha, kulukhuni manje; kumnyama phambili kanti nasemuva sekukude.  Usezenzile izifungo zokugcina.  Sekukhona nokuzisola ukuthi kodwa yena wabe engenwe yini ukuba

129

afise imali eningi kunalena abenenhlanhla ukuyithola ngomuthi lowo wezinkomo lezi esezondle umuzi wakubo?  Abamhluphi ngokucela imali oMaMadlala kanti nansi nendodakazi izincwadi zonke ziyayincoma ukuthi iyisilomo esikoleni ngokuba nekhanda elilula ... kambe yena uNomvula?  Yeka, esethi ubulala indodakazi leyo eyodwana, bangabuye bamthole omunye umntwana nanini!
Nokho ngoba nemali yakhe engu-R300 ayikhokhela ukuzokwethwasa akusekho ukuyibiza manje, okungcono sekuyobonakala khona phambili - icebo liyozakha.
Wasuka lapha eFlagstaff ngamabhasi aye amlahla eSayidi nakhona wadlula ngesitimela saye samehlisa eMzumbe.  Nakhona amthatha amabhasi ngoba esitobhini sakubo wehla lapho kuqundeka amehlo.  Uphethe ipotimende lakhe elinsundu elinezimpahla zakhe zokugqoka nokulala. kube yisimolo afake kusona imithi bese-ke kuba wujosaka wakhe wasehlombe angehlukani naw'o lapho elifake khona lelikhubalo lakhe nemithi elihambisana nayo.  Akasibeki ngisho phansi isikhwama lesi.
Lokhu nabantu baningana abehla kuleyobhasi, washesha wathola amantombazane okumthwalisa wawathembisa ingogo uma efika ekhaya.  Yena wasala nalojosaka wakhe.  Besahambe ibangana, nakhu esezithela kunina uMaMbhele naye ezivelela komunye umuzi oseduzane.  Wase ewakhokhela amantombazane esewayalela ukuthi aze afike anikeze uMaMadlala.  Kwaba kuhle kwadela nakhu esezohambisana naso isalukazi.
"Hawu impela ndodana kusobala ukuthi ngizokwethwasa uma kanti sengiphupha into yenzeke!" Sekuzikhalela uMaMbhele lapho sebehlangana nendodana.  Ayange ayigone, ajabule akhale izinyembezi.
"Bheka ngoba ungithola lapha nje bengizothenga imbuzi ngoba lonke lelisonto selokhu liqalile bengilokhu ngiphupha uyihlo ekhuluma ethi angikuhlangabeze ngokuhlaba lembuzi.  Sengize ngayithenga kanti nangempela ngoba nakhu futhi sewufikile uqobo lwakho." Kuzikhalela isalukazi simgona okwengane encane.  Siyefiluleka ngisho nawukufihla intokozo esinayo uma indodana yaso seyibuye unomphela njengokusho kwayo mhla begcinana.
"Kodwa khona ekhaya nisaphila nonke mama?" sekubuza yena uMndayiza efikelwa yifindo emphinjeni uma esekhu-

130

mbula amazwi abehlukane ngawo benoFikeni nenyanga leyo yabo.
"Kodwa wangibelesela ngendaba yempilo lokhu uyasibona siyaphila nje?  Mina engithanda ukukubuza Mndayiza ukuthi sewubuye unomphela manje?  Ngeke usaphindela eMaMpondweni?" Sekusho sona isalukazi simbuka sengathi kasikholwa wukuthi sibona yena uqobo lwakhe.
'Mama wami othandekayo, ungesabi lutho ngoba sengibuye unomphela.  Ngeke ngisasuka lapha phambi kwamehlo akho." Kuphendula uMndayiza naye ethuke sezigcwele amehlo.  Bakhale lapho begonene isikhashana.  Babuye futhi baqhubeke.
Amantombazane ahambe nempahla asesithele kude le; asefikile ngisho nakhona ekhaya.  Bona baze bafinyelela ekhaya sekuqundeke amehlo lokhu bahamba nje bayaxoxa futhi naso isalukazi asisakwazi ukuhamba sisheshe.
Bathi lapho sebezongena ekhaya, wase ephambuka uMndayiza naso lesikhwama sakhe sasehlombe esitshathwayo.  Uthe angathi tshobe emahlozini angenhlana nje komuzi,,wase esifihla khona lapho esethi ukuziba isikhashana ukuze kube sengathi ubengumuntu osaye kozikhulula.  Wase eseqonda khona exhibeni eseyobulisa lapha kumakoti nakundodakazi.
Kwabe kungeniswa intondolo leyo ebeyiye kothengwa wunina.  Balala kudliwe izibindi zayo ngalobobusuku kukuhle kudelile lapha kuMaMbhele.  Kade esemlandisa ukuthi imisebenzi kamalokazana iyancomeka ngoba abantu bafika lapha ekhaya bezochatha izingane zabo kanti nabanumzane bafika befikile bezofuna ukuba babethelelwe izibaya zabo.
"Ngisho noma sengingazunywa wukufa manje Mndayiza, mntanami, ngingeze ngakhala ngalutho ngoba nakhu sewubuyile.  Yini nje engingathi ngisayikhalela engingayibonanga emhlabeni?" sekusho sona isalukazi sihlengezela izinyembezi.  "Umakoti nangu, umzukulu uNomvula nangu uyaphila, nakhu nawe sewubuyile; pho ngingathi ngisakhala ngani kumdali uma engangithatha ngiye kokhonza koyihlo?"
Ukhuluma nje, lawomazwi ayahlaba lapha kuMndayiza.  Wazumeka lapho kwaba sengathi uthunyiselwe wudosi lwempisi.  Wazivukela ngakusasa nelanga seliphezulu nakhu ebika ukuthi ukhathazwe wuhambo lwabo lolo ngebhasi usuku lonke.

131

"Habe, yise kaNomvula, kanti muva nje sewulala sengathi ufile?" sekubuza umakoti esemlethele amanzi okugeza.  Kade yena evukile wayophemba exhibeni.
"Ungakusho ngani lokho nkosikazi lokhu bengiqwashile nj'e ngaze ngazumeka manje sekukhala izinkukhu?" kuphendula umnumzane ezamula ezelula.
"Musa wena ukukhuluma umhlola!  Bewuqwashe nini ngoba ngikuvuse ngaze ngadela ebusuku?  Pho manje bewuqwashe nini yise kaNomvula?" sekubabaza uMaMadlala eshaya izandla.  "Kungathi ngehlulekile ukukuvusa ngenkathi sibeleselwe wumsindo wembuzi emva kwendlu kodwa ungitshele ukuthi bewuqwashile?  Kanti ukuqwasha kushoni uma kungasho ukuphelelwa wubuthongo?"
"Yimbuzi ebeyikhalaphi leyo oyishoyo?  Mina angizwanga
mbuzi lapha." kulandula yena uMndayiza ephinda ezamula.
"Yekanini imihlola kayise kaNomvula!  Usho ukuthi awuyizwanga lembuzi ebeyibelesele ikhala emva kwendlu?" ambuke ngamanye amehlo manje umyeni wakhe.
"Kusobala yimbuzi yakubo kwalena ehlatshwe izolo.  Beyihamba ifuna yona." Sekuphendula uMndayiza lumuthi heqe uvalo.  Yake yakhala nanini imbuzi ebusuku?
"Habe, yise kaNomvula," sekusho umame lapho esemlethele umphungo wetiye lasekuseni," sona isikhwama sakho sikajosaka siphi namuhla?  Musa wena ukungitshela ukuthi wasithengisa lesiya sikhwama esihle kanjeya."
"Habe, nansi indaba ingikhulela bo!  Kanti lesosikhwama singesakho noma singesami?" washo ethi thwecu esigqikini ebheka ngasemnyango.  "Wangisiza wangikhumbuza ngoba bengisadinga ukuthi konje isikhwama sami uthi asisalanga nje lapho ngigcine ukuzikhululela khona?  Bheka ngoba sinyamalale nemithi emikhulu phakathi." Kusho yena uMndayiza ethatha izinyawo eyophuma ngomnyago.
"Musa wena ukukhuluma ngento ewumhlola!  Sewungakhohlwa yisikhwama sakho kanye nemithi yakho?" sekubabaza umakoti.  "Khona sewaba yisikhohlwa esadla impundu saze sayiphindelela, sewungakhohlwa yisikhwama emini libalele?"

Dukuduku ephumile, bayamethuka usebuya naso isikhwa-
ma leso.  Siyaconsa amazolo.
'Habe, yise kaNomvula kodwa awubulewe?  Isikhwama se-
132

singaze silale phandle sinemithi pho?" impela umakoti ambuke ngamanye amehlo.

Azithulele uMndayiza azibuzele uNomvula ukuthi ubengakavuki yini.  Phela kulemizuzwana ephumile, usefike walikhipha ikhubalo lapha esikhwameni ukuze alifihle ngaphandle komuzi.  Manje uselisusile lapha emva komuzi waye walishutheka ngasesibayeni.
Bayafika abantu bezombona, nalabo abaze nje bezofuna usizo.  Kwakuhle nje kudliwa nenyama leyo yentondolo kuphuzwa laze lashona ilanga.
Kwalalwa.  Hhayi-ke ngalobobusuku lokhu lendlu okulala khona oNomvula noninakhulu iyona egcine ngezansi ngasesibayeni, kwaze kwasa bebheke ngawayizolo.  Imbuzi manje seyikhala khona lapha ngasesibayeni eduze nesibaya samankonyane.

Ekuseni bavuswa yisona isalukazi sizikhalela ukuthi abazange kebalale ngenxa yomsindo lowo wembuzi ebeyikhala ngasesibayeni.

"Beyikhala kuze kube sengathi iklinyekile wumchilo," sekulanda uNomvula belandisa uyise.  "Ngimangele kabi ekuseni uma sengithi ngiyobheka ukuthi kodwa yona lembuzi beyikuphi.  Akubonakali ngisho nalapho beyikhulekwe khona."
"Cha, kulokhu ngiyizwile kodwa ngayizwela buthongweni ngaziduduza ngokuthi kungabe yizona izimbuzi zakubo kalena ehlatshwe kuthangi njengoba kade esho uyise kaNomvula." Sekusho uMaMadlala.
Ayizibe nje lendaba uMndayiza.  Abike ukuthi usazoke ahambe ngalelolanga usazoyodlulisa imiyalezo ayiphathiswe wufikeni ezihlotsheni.  Ngalobo busuku akazange abuye.  Lapha ekhaya isibani sakhanya kwaze kwasa ciki.  Bathi nje bangasicima, ibhoke imbuzi kuze kube sengathi seyikhala khona lapha emnyango wendlu ababelele khona ndawonye njengoba engekho uyise kaNomvula.
Ngenkathi ehambile uMndayiza kuthi ebusuku wahlangana nohlanya wangabe esakhuluma waluhlaba entanyeni ngommese walubulala.  Wase eludonsela ehlathini lapho afike waluhlinzela khona.  Wakhipha isibindi maqede wase eluphonsa esiweni ezihambela.  Akabuyanga nje ngoba ubesageza igazi lapha ezingutsheni.
Uma bemxoxela lendaba yembuzi ebeyibabelesele ngasesi-

133

bayeni, naye ubabaza ukuthi usinde ngokulambisa ehlaselwe
zigebengu.  Nebala bazibone nezingubo zakhe ukuthi cha
impela bekulukhuni.
"Nokho, ngenhlanhla, ngisizwe ukuthi nami bengihlomile ngazivikela ngabachitha." Sekusho yena uMndayiza.
"Phela ndodana izwe leli selagcwala izigcwelegcwele.  Ungalingi uhambe ebusuku kulezindawo zakini." Sekweluleka unina.
Kube seyedlule leyo.
Kungakalalwa, anyamalale futhi uMndayiza.  Manje phela usezohlanganisa isibindi leso sohlanya nekhubalo njengoba yabe ishilo inyanga ukuthi aze enze njani.  Kusihlwa bese elibuyisa ikhubalo esezolifaka lapha elawini labo.
Ngalobobusuku akazange akalugobe ukhophe uMaMadlala.  Manje imbuzi seyikhala khona lapha elawini!  Ikhala khona esikhwameni sikaMndayiza semithi!
Kwaba nje wukusicima isibani, sasuka isidumo.  Imbuzi seyikhala khona lapha endlini ibanga omkhulu umsindo.
"Cha, yise kaNomvula, mina angizuyimela lendaba yokungalali." Kubhoka uMaMadlala ehlala ngesinqe.  "Sala sewulikhuluma iqiniso lonke Ndimande.  Kanti yini lena osifikele nayo nalesikhwama sakho?  Selokhu ufikile, asibulali ubuthongo sibeleselwe yimbuzi ekhalayo.  Uma ngabe usibuyele nezimpundulu zaseMaMpondweni, mina anginakuyimela leyonto yokuba singalali.  Khuluma nje iqiniso lonke uma kuyinto edinga uyihlabele, uyihlabele."
Athule isikhathi eside uMndayiza ebheke phansi ngelikade aphendule athi:
Mfazi, akuyona indaba yakho leyo.  Yeka mina phansi uma ungafuni ngixabane nawe."
"Habe, usho ukuthi asisezukulala manje lapha ekhaya?" washo ethatha izingubo zokulala ephuma eyolala kuninazala.  Afike abaxoxele lendaba yembuzi eseyikhala endlini phakathi.  Naye uMndayiza angaze asicima isibani baze bazumeka endlini engezansi.
Ekuseni uma bevuki, kwakufika iveni yamaphoyisa izofuna yena uMndayiza ngoba sewutholakele umkhondo wegazi lohlanya lolo olwalutholwe lucwiywe isibindi.  Basiganklaza basiganklaza isicabha bethi akavule.  Phinde.  Baze basigqekeza bafica isidumbu sakhe uMndayiza naso sicwiywe isibindi.

134

Uma bephenya lapha esikhwameni, sitholakale isibindi sakhe kanye naleso sohlanya.
Amaphoyisa asithatha isidumbu sakhe sayohlolwa odokotela bakwaHulumeni.  Bamthatha naye uMaMadlala noMambhele ukuba bayobhalisa abakubonile nabakuzwile.
Uma seluphenywa yinkantolo udaba lokufa kukaMndayiza kwatholakala ukuthi ucwiywe 'umuntu noma abantu abangaziwa njengaye umufi okubonakala ukuthi wabe ecwiywe nguye uMndayiza."
Noma esashona uMaMbhele, kodwa uMaMadlala usaba yinyanga enkulu kanti uNomvula yena usephothule ezifundweni zobuhlengikazi esibhedlela.
